And I\'m definitely not saying that what they are doing is acceptable, but technically speaking, what they\'re doing or saying is not *PER SE* racist, because they have a problem with a certain religion, in this case Islam, not with a certain race*. (For example, anyone could become a christian, muslim, hindu or whatever, regardless of their ethnicity, skin color or "race".) They\'re what people would call "Islamophobic". And while Islamophobia or hate towards any other religion might not be the same as actual racism, that certainly doesn\'t necessarily mean that it\'s more or less acceptable than actual racism. So I\'m absolutely not saying that because it ain\'t racist, it suddenly becomes more acceptable. They\'re just not the same thing. You could compare it with Homophobia, which of course, isn\'t racism, but it\'s definitely not more acceptable that racism because of that.
